@HPV 
A MMU fault in the 2D Rasterizer usually indicates a problem with buffers used for 2D operations (copy or down-sample).
A MMU fault in the Copy Engine usually indicates a problem with buffer copies.
A MMU fault in the Graphics Processing Cluster may indicate texture fetch or other shader memory issues.
A MMU fault in the Host unit usually indicates Vulkan command buffer or D3D12 command list corruption issues.
A MMU fault in the Polymorph Engine usually indicates vertex buffer issues.
A MMU fault in the Primitive Distributor usually indicates index buffer issues.
A regular expression cannot start with the alternation operator |.
